The `stringformat` filter is registered with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`. This means Django's template auto-escaping considers this filter as \"safe\", which means the output is treated as safe HTML and won't be escaped further.\n\nSo the issue is:1. When you use `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` in a Django template with auto-escaping enabled2. The stringformat filter is marked as `is_safe=True`3. This means the output of stringformat is treated as safe, preventing further auto-escaping4.
